  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_aec898e4-579c-4c1e-b89a-48541f3dda49'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText16400850406410793989" style="display:none">Secrets. <br />Everyone has one. <br />Some are bigger than others. <br />And when secrets are revealed, <br />Some will heal you ... <br />And some will end you. <br /> <br />Kate Sedgwick’s life has been anything but typical. Kate is strong-willed, funny, smart, and musically gifted. She’s also never believed in love. So when Kate leaves San Diego to attend college in the small town of Grant, Minnesota, the last thing she expects is to fall in love with Keller Banks. <br /> <br />They both feel it. <br />But they each have a reason to fight it. <br />They each have a secret. <br /> <br />And when secrets are revealed, <br />Some will heal you … <br />And some will end you. <br /></span>

I highly recommend for you to read especially if you like tear jerker books. The build up of the characters are good. The flow of the story is great. I felt Every.single.emotions in this book. The author will capture your heart and make you feel you were part of the story. Yes, it is one of those books that you want to be there and live in it. Have a box of tissue ready when you read this. I'm not gonna spoil anything for you but look at the bright side ;)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433409702i/15093247.jpg' alt=' photo caa54133-4b3f-4b31-b8fc-6289fe88802f_zps1jmeshmi.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“We all have to fight to make the most of the life we're given.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br/>One of my co-bloggers/friends told me about this book when it was first released. It was her favorite book of last year and one of her favorite books of all time. I knew it would be good, but I dragged me feet when it came to reading it. Why you might ask? I knew the subject matter would be sensitive for me so I put it off. Then I put it off some more. When I saw it was available on audio, I thought</span>
  <span id="freeText1466189540452878934" style="display:none"><b>5+ Do Epic stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/caa54133-4b3f-4b31-b8fc-6289fe88802f_zps1jmeshmi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433409702i/15093247.jpg" alt=" photo caa54133-4b3f-4b31-b8fc-6289fe88802f_zps1jmeshmi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“We all have to fight to make the most of the life we're given.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>One of my co-bloggers/friends told me about this book when it was first released. It was her favorite book of last year and one of her favorite books of all time. I knew it would be good, but I dragged me feet when it came to reading it. Why you might ask? I knew the subject matter would be sensitive for me so I put it off. Then I put it off some more. When I saw it was available on audio, I thought now is the time to take the plunge. (A shout out to the female narrator (Lidia Dornet) she nailed Kate. Voiced her perfectly.) I’m so happy I did. For a story that was so sad at times, it had the best messages of DO EPIC and BE BRAVE. It was depressing at moments, but at the same time strangely positive. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/f73b2f4d-64cd-49a6-ac33-23686dd0ad57_zpsr5nou8b3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433409702i/15093248.jpg" alt=" photo f73b2f4d-64cd-49a6-ac33-23686dd0ad57_zpsr5nou8b3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t want to spoil the story for anyone so I’m just going to take some time to talk about the characters. <b>Kate</b> is one of the best heroines I’ve ever read about. She is that girl you want to be. She’s positive, always looks at the bright side of things no matter how bad they get, and she is funny. This girl made me laugh so many times. I love that she was never afraid to be herself. She never wanted to change to fit in or to be anything other than she was. She is a character that inspires. I read lots of books and ‘meet’ lots of characters but there are very few I can say inspire me to want to be better. To want to make positive changes in my life. When a book can have that effect, it’s pretty special.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/7ddc8d8c-ddd3-45b7-b748-c02fd78897fe_zpsawxifuro.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433409702i/15093249.jpg" alt=" photo 7ddc8d8c-ddd3-45b7-b748-c02fd78897fe_zpsawxifuro.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Not only was Kate a wonderful character, but there were a slue of other amazing characters in this book. Keller was great of course. And I loved her friends Shelley, Clayton, Pete, Duncan and the entire band of Rook. But there was this one character of the story that stood out to me above others. From the beginning he was an instant favorite just like Kate. And his name is <b>Gus</b>. Gus has been Kate’s best friend since childhood. They have a special relationship. One of hugs, I love you’s, constant skyping and dude’s. Gus is touring with his band while Kate is living her college/life journey but he is still a huge part of her life and the book. I am ecstatic to read his story that was just released!<br><br>I love emotional books. I don’t mind when they make me cry, make me feel and get under my skin. But I love that this book also made me smile so big, made me laugh, and genuinely made me happy and look at life in a different light. This book had all of that. It made me break down and cry. It devastated me at times. But it was SO worth it. Bright Side isn’t just a story you read, it’s a story you live. So grab a cup of black coffee, listen to some good music and get ready to Do Epic. This book will be going right on my favorites list and I highly recommend it to all. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/38ec3e22-d2db-4a01-a19e-cd715c4abd29_zpszhh9ofxv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433409702i/15093250.jpg" alt=" photo 38ec3e22-d2db-4a01-a19e-cd715c4abd29_zpszhh9ofxv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12509299263549463249"><b>4.5~Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Dude, I can't even….</b><br/><br/>It has been days. Days!! I just can't, but I gotta. But I can't. I must. <br/><br/>Numbness. Feels. Overload. <br/><br/>It's impossible. <br/><br/>Here I go.<br/><br/>I'm going.<br/><br/>Okay.<br/><br/>So.<br/><br/>Maybe it would be best if I started at the beginning. <br/><br/>It all started as a goodreads recommendation….from Donna. <i>Donna</i>. The person I want to hug. Punch in the face. Hug. Punch. Damn you! You owe me valium…and ice cream. After the recommendation, I read the synopsis. Intriguing. I also loved the fact that it only had three rev</span>
  <span id="freeText12509299263549463249" style="display:none"><b>4.5~Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Dude, I can't even….</b><br /><br />It has been days. Days!! I just can't, but I gotta. But I can't. I must. <br /><br />Numbness. Feels. Overload. <br /><br />It's impossible. <br /><br />Here I go.<br /><br />I'm going.<br /><br />Okay.<br /><br />So.<br /><br />Maybe it would be best if I started at the beginning. <br /><br />It all started as a goodreads recommendation….from Donna. <i>Donna</i>. The person I want to hug. Punch in the face. Hug. Punch. Damn you! You owe me valium…and ice cream. After the recommendation, I read the synopsis. Intriguing. I also loved the fact that it only had three reviews. I absolutely love new unknowns. It's like a secret. <i>My</i> secret. I decided to give it a go.<br /><br />I went. <br /><br />There's no going back. <br /><br />These feelings can't be unfelt.<br /><br />I feel.<br /><br />Kate Sedgwick may be one of my favorite female characters of all time. Let's face it, female characters usually have the tendency to be….well, they sometimes suck. They're annoying. I usually prefer the male characters. I don't play well with others. <br /><br />Wait! <br /><br />Before you revoke my woman card or force me to burn my bra and roar, it's kind of a common occurrence with female heroines. They frustrate. They annoy. <br /><br />I'm sure the nations leading psychologists might theorize that my "issues" with female characters probably stem from a place of jealousy. Damn straight. They never deserve the guy. My guy. I tolerate them because without them, there'd be no story.<br /><br />Not Kate. I more than tolerated Kate. I adored Kate. I loved Kate. I was tied to everything she felt, experienced. Her character is unforgettable. This story is unforgettable. <br /><br />I feel.<br /><br />Then there's Gus (who I hear is getting his own book), and Keller, and Clayton, and Stella, and pretty much every character in this book.<br /><br />I. Can't. Even.<br /><br />The love between Gus and Bright Side. The love between her and Keller. I felt everything. The love was intoxicating. Suffocating. It hurt. It healed.<br /><br />Sure the plot was predictable, but nothing. Nothing, prepared me for the emotions. I started crying during the last half, sobbed my way through the final chapters, but somehow I ended the book with a smile. <br /><br />The hurt and emotions didn't cause me to break. I endured. I survived. Each emotion was coupled with humor, wit, an amazing story, and unforgettable characters. Laugh. Cry. Heal. <br /><br />Embark on this incredible journey.<br /><br />DO EPIC!<br /><br />More reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1040016060" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1040016060" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1040016060?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22673436-bright-side">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rock-stars">rock-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1040016060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17761276646504102150">This book wrecked me! It was incredibly touching and heartfelt. Despite dealing with some rather depressing subject matter, it was handled with care. I can't say that I didn't cry big fat tears, but I can say that I smiled far more than I cried while reading this book. It was beautiful.<br/><br/>The heroine, Kate, moves from San Diego to Grant, Minnesota for college. Right off the bat, I loved her. It is easy to understand why her best friend, Gus, gave her the nickname "Bright Side". She is the type of p</span>
  <span id="freeText17761276646504102150" style="display:none">This book wrecked me! It was incredibly touching and heartfelt. Despite dealing with some rather depressing subject matter, it was handled with care. I can't say that I didn't cry big fat tears, but I can say that I smiled far more than I cried while reading this book. It was beautiful.<br /><br />The heroine, Kate, moves from San Diego to Grant, Minnesota for college. Right off the bat, I loved her. It is easy to understand why her best friend, Gus, gave her the nickname "Bright Side". She is the type of person that just lights up a room. Kudos to the narrator for being able to capture the essence of Kate's character so well.<br /><br />As Kate makes friends in her new home, she never lets her relationship with Gus weaken. They talk daily on the phone, while he tours with his band, Rook. There is no mistaking the strength of their bond, or the fact that there are feelings shared that extend beyond the bounds of normal friendship.<br /><br />Despite claiming not to believe in romantic love, Kate finds herself falling in love. Keller Banks is the hot guy that works the counter at the coffee shop that she frequents for her caffeine fix. They flirt tirelessly and find themselves thrown together more often through mutual friends. <br /><br />Once Kate and Keller begin spending more time together, their attraction is evident. Before long, Keller has let Kate into the private aspects of his life that he doesn't share with others. The two grow incredibly close in a very short period of time. <br /><br />Nobody is more surprised by their quick intimacy than Kate herself. She never planned on falling in love. She didn't even believe it existed. More importantly, she has a big secret that she's been keeping from everyone she loves, which she knows will ruin everything.<br /><br />Aside from the romance between Kate and Keller, I found myself drawn to the stories of friendship in this book. Kate's relationship with Gus was incredible. The support and love between them was so strong it was tangible. Similarly, her relationships with Clayton, Shelley and Pete were inspiring. <br /><br />This book certainly did not lack for a strong cast of supporting characters. Each of these characters was endearing in their own way. Even the ones that made me mad initially, like Kate's roommate, won me over eventually. I loved all of them and am looking forward to reading their stories.<br /><br />In the end, I cried big, fat tears. It was sad, but also very inspiring. This is one of those books that makes you step back and reevaluate how you go through life. It was inspirational and helps keep things in perspective. <br /><br />This is a must-read! I can't believe that I put it off for so long, but I am so glad that I finally read it. This book was fabulous! </span>

<div id="review_1227197238" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1227197238" />
    <a title="Seth King" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34814076-seth-king"><img alt="Seth King" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420995275p2/34814076.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1227197238?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Seth King" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Seth King" href="/user/show/34814076-seth-king">Seth King</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1227197238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7252937448939155921">First of all: I get it.<br/><br/>To all the people out there who say they don’t like these types of books, books that make you hurt and feel and clutch your Kindle at 3 AM as tears blur your vision and you hope against hope that the character isn't headed towards what you think they're headed towards: I get it.<br/><br/>Life is hard. This world is a tough place. Crappy things are happening out there, things that break your heart on the evening news, and sometimes it’s easier to just drift along and float above the </span>
  <span id="freeText7252937448939155921" style="display:none">First of all: I get it.<br /><br />To all the people out there who say they don’t like these types of books, books that make you hurt and feel and clutch your Kindle at 3 AM as tears blur your vision and you hope against hope that the character isn't headed towards what you think they're headed towards: I get it.<br /><br />Life is hard. This world is a tough place. Crappy things are happening out there, things that break your heart on the evening news, and sometimes it’s easier to just drift along and float above the clouds than to actually sink down deep and risk getting hurt. There’s enough pain out there – why run towards more, right?<br /><br />But Bright Side is worth the pain. In Kate and Keller, Kim Holden has created two remarkable characters, and after you’re drawn in through their banter and connection, you do start to fear for the worst. You start to fear that you’ll be that person hurting and feeling and clutching your tear-stained Kindle as you pray that The Almighty Worst won't happen. And when it does, it feels less like facing a gust of wind on a winter day than getting swamped by a frozen wave in the dead of January. And that's not fun. For anyone.<br /><br />But that’s what makes us human, right? That’s what separates us from the rodents and the beasts and the swine, isn't it? We are elegant creatures capable of depth and empathy and heartbreak, who clutch Kindles and hurt and feel – especially at 3 AM. <br /><br />Especially in the hands of Kim Holden.<br /><br />Epically done, Kim.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7252937448939155921" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1543771348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16098359208426613982">What would you do if you found it that you had only six months to live ?<br/>Would you clean out your account and go about doing things on your bucket list. Would you throw a pity party and expect all of your near and dear ones to come be with you as you spend at precious moments on this earth. Would you leave quietly and hide out so you don't see sadness in the eyes of your beloved people and it'll break your heart?. What will you do in the last month...week...day...hours ?<br/>Or would you touch all the</span>
  <span id="freeText16098359208426613982" style="display:none">What would you do if you found it that you had only six months to live ?<br />Would you clean out your account and go about doing things on your bucket list. Would you throw a pity party and expect all of your near and dear ones to come be with you as you spend at precious moments on this earth. Would you leave quietly and hide out so you don't see sadness in the eyes of your beloved people and it'll break your heart?. What will you do in the last month...week...day...hours ?<br />Or would you touch all the people's lives with fun and humour and kindness and love.open heated , all encompassing love<br />Kate sedgwick took the choice to #DoEpic.<br />that's what kim created. A masterpiece, a story so intense that it shames you for being petty and whiny when your car breaks down or you miss out on a sale or you fight with your family or you yell at your kids or when you're stuck in traffic...<br />life is all about Sunsets and people ! Time to be with people you love and share beautiful moments with them like sunsets , or coffee, or books or music or just tShirts.<br />This book made me bawl hard...and I mean HARD ! It reminded me today to smile at strangers a little more widely , love my husband a little more intensely , hug my son a little more tightly . I never know whose life I may be touching today, making it a teeny bit better . I wanna be Kate now, today , tomorrow . Shes an intensely powerful, brave strong girl who captures everyone's heart , her purity of soul and generous spirit spellbinds everyone who she touches. Kim has created the perfect girl warrior. Some kind of a hero , who I aspire to be .😊<br />Kim writes -<br />" don’t forsake the present for the unknowns of the future. A lot of happiness is bypassed, overlooked, postponed to a time years from now that may never come. Don’t bide your time and miss out on this moment for a tomorrow with no guarantee.”<br />I promise to #DoEpic<br />sunsets and people, thats what its all about 💖<br />#BookBistroBlogApproved <br />Follow me on:<br />BookBistroBlog@gmail.com<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://Twitter.com/BookBistro">https://Twitter.com/BookBistro</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.instagram.com/BookBistroBlog">www.instagram.com/BookBistroBlog</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bookbistroblogger.blogspot.com/">https://bookbistroblogger.blogspot.com/</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/BookBistroBlog">https://www.facebook.com/groups/BookB...</a></span>

<div id="review_1041091999" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1041091999" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1041091999?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=turtles-are-slow">turtles-are-slow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1041091999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer122364862119759764"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409595365i/10996991._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’ve been on an angst-fest/emotional kick lately so when I saw the blurb for <u>Bright Side,</u> I knew it was a book I wanted to read ASAP. Now that I’ve finished it, the first thing that popped up in my mind was <i>well, that wasn’t what I expected.</i> Honestly, if it wasn’t for the last 25% of the book that completely blew me away, I would’ve given this book 2 stars. That being said though, the heroine is a pretty refreshing character and the dry humor and sarcasm present in the book were things</span>
  <span id="freeText122364862119759764" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409595365i/10996991._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’ve been on an angst-fest/emotional kick lately so when I saw the blurb for <u>Bright Side,</u> I knew it was a book I wanted to read ASAP. Now that I’ve finished it, the first thing that popped up in my mind was <i>well, that wasn’t what I expected.</i> Honestly, if it wasn’t for the last 25% of the book that completely blew me away, I would’ve given this book 2 stars. That being said though, the heroine is a pretty refreshing character and the dry humor and sarcasm present in the book were things I could appreciate. <br><br>************************<br><br>The heroine <b>Kate Sedgwick</b> (or should I call her Katie, Katherine, or ‘Bright Side?’) has had a hard life. Having a mother who didn’t care much for her children, a father who left, and a sister who passed away, Kate should technically be cynical and emotionally closed off to everybody but she isn’t. For some inexplicable reason, she remains rather optimistic about everything and becomes a ‘bright side’ to everyone she meets (more on that later). Leaving her closest friend Gus behind, Kate heads off to college and meets the guy she never expects to meet. <br><br><b>Keller Banks</b> is first introduced as the charming guy who works at the coffee shop near campus. When Kate and Keller meet, rainbows shine brightly – both recognize that seeing each other ignites something in them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409595365i/10996992._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the book progresses and their relationship develops slowly, both of their hidden secrets (that the reader is privy to) are revealed and that completely changes their relationship dynamic. <br><br>************************<br><br>To start with, the first 65% of the book was just plain boring. There were occasional laughs on my part but most of the time I would be asking myself why the heck am I not DNFing this?? I also had a hard time warming up to the heroine. Not that I didn’t love how refreshing her character was but sometimes I felt like the author was laying it on too thick with all the sarcasm it became an overkill. Additionally, there was a lack of buildup…to everything actually. Kellar and Kate’s relationship moved as fast as a turtle for the first 50% and then all of a sudden this insanely intense chemistry appears and bam, they’re finally together. There was also little to no buildup in regards to their secrets. It’s pretty obvious what Kate’s hiding because there are big clues in the first few chapters but after that, there is no mention of it again until it’s revealed. It comes out in a way that seems rushed and on the spot, giving the reader no time to adjust to the event. But despite knowing what she was hiding, I <i>still</i> got all emotional and teary-eyed in the last 25% witnessing the aftermath. Then I pretty much ugly cried when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[all the letters were being read out loud. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409595365i/10996993._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Would I recommend this?</b> I really don’t know now. If you aren’t a fan of extremely slow books maybe you should skip over this one. But if you’re willing to endure massive boredom to get to the heartfelt, touching part of the story, maybe this one is for you. My favorite part of the book was seeing all the lives Kate touched and brightened, and I say this with the most sincerity I have: I truly am looking forward to Gus’s story. Just make it more fast-paced than this one PLEASE!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="122364862119759764" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1280282338" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15060041390901089817"><b>6++++++ #DoEpic #BeBrave Stars</b><br/> <br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/513CCE02-A9CF-4904-8895-099E10317727_zps6gc1egix.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432643823i/14993242._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 513CCE02-A9CF-4904-8895-099E10317727_zps6gc1egix.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/>Reading is my getaway, my sanctuary I have a busy life and don't we all? But reading is my <b>Me</b> time. I love reading and I have read a lot of books this year so far saying that no insults to anyone here but this has been my <b>FAVOURITE Read</b> of the year so far this book is a book of life and living, friendship <b>LOVE</b> all in one. I know that a lot know what the story entails but for those who don't I'm going to try my best to keep my thoughts as <b>SPOILER FREE</b> as possib</span>
  <span id="freeText15060041390901089817" style="display:none"><b>6++++++ #DoEpic #BeBrave Stars</b><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/513CCE02-A9CF-4904-8895-099E10317727_zps6gc1egix.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432643823i/14993242._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 513CCE02-A9CF-4904-8895-099E10317727_zps6gc1egix.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Reading is my getaway, my sanctuary I have a busy life and don't we all? But reading is my <b>Me</b> time. I love reading and I have read a lot of books this year so far saying that no insults to anyone here but this has been my <b>FAVOURITE Read</b> of the year so far this book is a book of life and living, friendship <b>LOVE</b> all in one. I know that a lot know what the story entails but for those who don't I'm going to try my best to keep my thoughts as <b>SPOILER FREE</b> as possible. <br> <br><b>Gah I'm speechless ack ummmm I DON'T EVEN errr know where to start?</b><br>Ok lets start from the beginning, we have a beautiful bright character that literally loves the world NO wrong word she loves <b>LIFE</b> she loves to breathe the air and she takes every day as a new day she enjoys every moment, everything she does or creates is with purpose to <b>LOVE</b> she takes chances on everything, you know when you walk past a person and you think that guy could do with a friend? or that mum could do with a hug and tell them everything's going to be OK? well that's Kate she takes life in her stride, she takes chances and she makes people smile she teaches the people around her how to <b>LOVE</b> freely. You know the world would be a bright better place if we had more Kate's and Katie's in the world, LOL sorry that's my name isn't it? no pun intended here #JustSaying. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/6A59DF28-7608-4386-945C-7D2E6E45D51E_zpsc0r46ct1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432585966i/14984965._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6A59DF28-7608-4386-945C-7D2E6E45D51E_zpsc0r46ct1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Bright Side is the most generous loving talented and <i>Beautiful</i> young lady to read, I connected with her straight away. For me there was just something that made me think and ,while reading, breathe the way she did. <br> <br>She is starting a new chapter in her life though she has moved away from her home and is now at university just about the start her new course in training to become a Special Needs Teacher. <br>But she is moving away from her best friend whom she has known and been with her whole life. Gus has been pretty much present along her side for every first and every moment they have been together, therefore to begin with life is strange , still good but different. <br> <br><b>Lets talk about Gus for a minute</b><br>Gus Gus Gustov my heart melted for him, his Intense loving nature, you can't do anything but love him. He's the lead singer of the Band Rook and he's starting his career as a musician. The Rock Band is a rising and Gus is touring with the other members on the road therefore Kate and Gus's relationship are of phone calls , texts throughout the day and then skype sessions every so often . Those Skype sessions were some of my favourite moments at the beginning that's all I'm saying there were some serious #Sigh moments between them.<br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/A2CAF140-A680-47DD-8886-E57043536ACA_zpsegczu1fx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432643823i/14993243._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo A2CAF140-A680-47DD-8886-E57043536ACA_zpsegczu1fx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>Their relationship is unique to say the least</b><br> <br>There is something that Kate loves more than life and that is STRONG BLACK COFFEE and therefore a coffee shop is needed not just Starbucks or Costa <b>Nope</b> she wants a cosy down to earth heartily coffee shop that has <b>normal</b> coffee and that's where she meets <b>Keller</b>. <br>First attractions are something that are new to Bright Side she's taken with Keller instantly and their relationship blossoms gradually. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/0788FE92-BAEE-4C10-878D-B53F9292FDD3_zpsfk3ujxbm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432643823i/14993244._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0788FE92-BAEE-4C10-878D-B53F9292FDD3_zpsfk3ujxbm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>I'm not going to say anything else other than this book is <b>The Book Of Life</b> no joke it touched me more than anything I've read in a long long time. Saying that it may not be for everyone this is a No smut read this is an emotional journey and the first half is a slower intimate start where Kim has weaved so many people into Kate's life gradually and somehow surrounded Kate with a circle of friends who become her life. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/9369D1F0-D640-44B2-8177-3C8CE0AFF7DA_zpsv1rdt7iu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432643824i/14993245._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9369D1F0-D640-44B2-8177-3C8CE0AFF7DA_zpsv1rdt7iu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>I'm not going to say anything else other than Kim Holden is an <b>Genius</b> she really is, this is a NA read and although it was a gradual process I had time to get to know each person individually and together it meant in the last half I had a close connection to what was happening and why I was so emotionally involved in the last half. Kim's writing is just exquisite and you feel like you're there with each and everyone of them. <br> <br><b>For me</b> this was a life changing book, it made me think and be happy to be where I am that I have a big loving family that I'm so very happy to be part of. I have a few very close friends that are special to me, if your a real life friend or I've met here on Goodreads mainly by Blog Besties Shannie &amp; Elizabeth and my Girl Layla I love you guys to the moon and back your all important to me in some way or another. I have a job where I can care and eventually go back and train (when my girls are all in school) to become a qualified nurse and do something where I feel like I've made a difference, it made me realise how very lucky I am to be surrounded by good people, it made me want to <b>LIVE</b> the moments and #DoEpics daily. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/E78109F1-16B9-4CE7-946C-D490D31A02B7_zpsemfak8ba.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432643824i/14993246._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo E78109F1-16B9-4CE7-946C-D490D31A02B7_zpsemfak8ba.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>READ THIS BOOK</b> <br> <br><b>Song list for anyone who like me needed to listen as well as read this is the songs I followed on Spotifty</b><br> <br>We Might Be Dead By Tomorrow ~ Soko. Thought I Was An Alien <br>400 Lux ~ Lorde.Pure Heroine<br>Eula ~ Baroness. Yellow &amp; Green<br>Sleeping Witch ~ Royal Thunder.CVI<br>Jump Into The Fog ~ The Wombats<br>Bug Eyes ~ Dredg. Catch Without Arms<br>Done With Love ~Teenage Bottlerocket. Freak Out!<br>Waiting All Night(Feat. Ella Eyre). Rudimental<br>Same Love-feat. Mary Lambert<br>Mutilate Me ~ Teenage Bottlerocket. Freak Out!<br>Lullaby ~ The Cure. Greatest Hits<br>Angels ~ The xx. Coexist<br>My Song 5 ~ Halm. Days Are Gone<br>Sex ~ The 1975<br>Panic Switch ~ Silversun Pickups. Swoon<br>Sweater Weather ~ The Neighbourhood. <br>Nothing Left To Say/Rocks ~ Imagine Dragons. Night Visions<br>Northern Lights ~ Thirty Seconds To Mars<br>Pictures Of You ~ The Cure. Galore<br>Let Her Go ~ Passenger. All the little lights<br>Everything To Nothing ~ Manchester Orchestra<br>Favor's Keeper ~ Index Case.   <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1041842919" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11119751534300979134">5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance<br/>	<br/><b>My my my…what a read! Slow easy beginning, <i>AMAZINGLY</i> beautiful ending! I did not give this book 5 STARS it<i> SNATCHED </i>the 5 STARS right out of my hands.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073324.jpg' alt=' photo 85b3210b-888c-4737-93ed-7937ed5ff12c_zpsf5682e0c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073323.jpg' alt=' photo brightsidefinalpic3_zps3b1e5f09.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Kate Sedgwick has faced<b> many</b> adversities in her young life thus far; having a mother who was not so motherly and in addition a sister Grace, to care for all on her own... Instead of cowering in fear at the cards life dealt Katie did what she had to do, she grew up fast. When the book starts Kate is about to </span>
  <span id="freeText11119751534300979134" style="display:none">5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br>	<br><b>My my my…what a read! Slow easy beginning, <i>AMAZINGLY</i> beautiful ending! I did not give this book 5 STARS it<i> SNATCHED </i>the 5 STARS right out of my hands.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073324.jpg" alt=" photo 85b3210b-888c-4737-93ed-7937ed5ff12c_zpsf5682e0c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073323.jpg" alt=" photo brightsidefinalpic3_zps3b1e5f09.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Kate Sedgwick has faced<b> many</b> adversities in her young life thus far; having a mother who was not so motherly and in addition a sister Grace, to care for all on her own... Instead of cowering in fear at the cards life dealt Katie did what she had to do, she grew up fast. When the book starts Kate is about to start college in the small town of Grant Minnesota; leaving behind her best friend Gus and the sunny skies of San Diego, California. <br><br>As Katie adjusts to Grant she moves into the dorms and makes a new friend along the way, Clayton. Whom by the way I LOVE!!! Eventually she decides to seek out coffee to feed her daily addiction. Her search leads her to Grounds where she befriends the owner. With his help she lands a job that same day.<br><br> It’s not long before I realize that there is something special about Katie. She has the power to change a person…an atmosphere… I can’t even explain it. I guess the best way to say it is that Katie impacts lives. You don’t meet her without a mark being left. Her presence is almost enchanting because the second she opens her mouth she has your attention with her witticisms and sass. <br><br>It's not long before one trip to Grounds changes everything. Katie meets Keller Banks an easy going extremely HOT guy working the counter. A semi flirty verbal spar over coffee ensues. Eventually after spending time as friends Keller makes his intentions clear in a very sweet and <i>swoon</i> worthy way.<br><br><b>
  <i> “Keller. What is this, birthday week ? This isn’t necessary. You took me out for dinner last night, remember?” <br>He shrugs. “That was from all of us .” He smiles sweetly . “This is from me.”<br> I open it. It’s a twenty-dollar gift card to Grounds. “Thanks. It’s perfect.” Thinking back to our conversation a few weeks ago at the flower shop, I add, “Is this blackmail or bribery?” <br>“Neither. It’s insurance.” <br>“Insurance?”<br>“Yeah. That’s twelve cups of coffee . Twelve trips to Grounds . Twelve chances to see you.” </i>
</b><br><br>Soon Katie finds herself falling for Keller; and as much as she tries to keep it platonic between them he still breaks through her walls and gains entrance to her heart. Seeing that her defenses are ineffectual towards him she gives in.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073325.jpg" alt=" photo Brightsidefinalpic2_zps8d5caa9f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After enduring hardships no one should have to face Katie’s optimistic outlook in life had her coined as Bright Side by her best friend Gus. Gus is very protective of Katie and with good reason; she has one of the biggest kindest hearts you could ever come across. So when you realize that she is hiding something important you feel a bit slighted. <br><br>Only she’s not the only one holding secrets…Keller has a few as well.<br><br>Life changing secrets…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073326._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BrightSidefinalpic1_zps39df9bf5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Just when you think you know someone, they change. Or you change. Or maybe you both change. And that changes everything.</b>
</i> -Keller<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410199843i/11073327.jpg" alt=" photo brightsidefinalpic4_zps23468436.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>FAVE SCENE</b>
</u> <br><br><i>'He’s not yelling at me, he’s yelling with me.'</i> -Katie <br>(You have to read the scene to understand let’s just say I wept right here)<br><br>There is also a scene with Gus and Keller that I LOVE!!! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410199843ra/11073328.gif" alt=" photo hearts_zps2cbeef3d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>HUGE SHOUT OUT TO <b>Donna</b> at The Romance Cover and <b>Jenny</b> at Totally Booked for recommending this to me! <br><br>OH MY GAWD! Where to start? Kate, let’s start there. In one word I would describe Kate as jovial, always of good cheer and humorous at heart. The second she speaks people listen whether they like what is coming out of her mouth or not. She's also ballsy, which I loved! She has the lovingly precious friendship with Gus that just melted my heart. There is SO MUCH I want to say about him but I won’t. You need to meet him for yourself, trust me he will not disappoint. If I know anything I know this. Readers will want MORE OF GUS!!<br><br><u>The Writing</u> -The book has a slow start as you go through the everyday small routines of a college girl. <b>HOWEVER </b> in these small mundane daily tasks Katie is causing these small tremors in the lives of those she comes in contact with. It may be small, like a song choice that pulls a smile out of someone who rarely smiles. OR it could be big and courageous like standing up for what’s right in a world filled with people who prefer to duck and look the other way. <br><br>At a certain point the book will take the air right out of your lungs rendering you BREATHLESS. Don’t let that stop you, keep reading.<br><br>I like Kim Holden’s style; she’s always <b>saying</b> something or maybe I should say relaying something about Kate in her writing when you’re not looking for it… its genius really. Pay attention tell me if you catch it. Watch the impressions Kate leaves on those around her. Yeah…I really dig Kim Holden’s writing style. Her words are well thought out and served with a purpose. Am I the only one who caught that? (Question is posed to readers)<br><br><u>My Ratings</u><br><b>Characters-</b> Lovable, Sweet, Endearing and HOT <br><b>Writing Style-</b> Strong and Methodical, which most won’t understand but it is, EVERY word served a purpose as I previously stated.<br><b>Plot/Storyline-</b> A girl leaves Cali to go attend college in a small Minnesota town where she makes new friends and finds LOVE.<br><b>Steam Factor-</b> High/Very Steamy on a scale of 1-10 I say 8 BTW, the steam came out of nowhere. HIT ME LIKE A HUGE WAVE OF FLAMES! <br><b>Entertainment Level-</b> Lo-Med-Hi I say Medium, the book held my attention, pulled out a few laughs and caused some big grins to spread across my face.<br><b>Overall-</b> I LOVED IT! I HIGHLY Recommend you read it!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br><b>For more reviews got to:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot...</a> <br><b>Like us on Facebook:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/realitybitesletsgetlost">www.facebook.com/realitybitesletsgetlost</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11119751534300979134" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1085519947" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1085519947" />
    <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b"><img alt="M. ~ B&amp;B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435261660p2/14479657.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1085519947?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M. ~ B&amp;B" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b">M. ~ B&amp;B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22673436-bright-side">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1085519947" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14226811461397509111">So I finished this and I am not impressed.<br/><br/>You know that feeling that you get when you read the first line or the first chapter of the book and you just <i>know</i> you are going to love what you're reading and never want to put it down? Yeah, Bright Side had the opposite effect. I started reading and I was like, okay, maybe this could be good, but the writing is a bit off. Then I read a few more chapters and was like, okay, where is this going... (from the beginning I already figured out the premise: p</span>
  <span id="freeText14226811461397509111" style="display:none">So I finished this and I am not impressed.<br /><br />You know that feeling that you get when you read the first line or the first chapter of the book and you just <i>know</i> you are going to love what you're reading and never want to put it down? Yeah, Bright Side had the opposite effect. I started reading and I was like, okay, maybe this could be good, but the writing is a bit off. Then I read a few more chapters and was like, okay, where is this going... (from the beginning I already figured out the premise: perfect girl who always sees everything from the Bright Side and helps everyone around her out <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[before she dies <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>). But the storytelling was all over the place. Seriously, it was a day by day account of a 19 year old (overly positive) girl starting college in a new place. It's bo-ring with all the typical cheesy stuff, including the gay (best) friend, the slutty roommate, the new love interest and the badass friend who is nothing like her but they get along. It's constant phone calls with the best friend, dinners with the bitchy aunt, late night dancing with the new gay friend, getting coffee from a super hot guy who she fell in insta-lust with, getting locked out of her own dorm room by her slutty roommate, and working with a girl who is super closed-off, but she becomes instant best friends with after sharing music. And this goes on and on in repeat until about 60-70%. So where the fuck is this going, really? By the time it was supposed to get interesting, I was so damn bored and so detached from the characters, that I didn't really care.<br /><br />I didn't cry. Not one single tear. That is how disconnected I felt. The book, to me, was very cliché, typical and unoriginal. And sometimes I can get over that, if there are other redeeming qualities. Which there weren't. The writing was very mediocre, the relationships between the characters felt very unnatural (this is a huge factor that attributed to the disconnection), and I rolled my eyes way too many times. For the most part I could just copy my review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/693049608" rel="nofollow noopener">Ruin</a> here. <br /><br />So I don't know why I gave this 3 stars. I wanted to give it 2 stars, but felt like maybe that's a bit too harsh, because I downright hated some books and rated those 2 stars too. I just felt very indifferent towards this book and I don't feel like I would've missed out on anything had I not read it. The last 25% was supposed to save the book (it's why I didn't DNF), but all I did was roll my eyes even more then. It was so annoying and unrealistic how perfect Kate was set out to be. She's so brave, so strong, so drop-dead gorgeous, so caring, so loving, so talented, so smart, so positive, so kind, and so on. By the end, every one of her friends were all like "Kate's the best thing that ever happened in my life." Annoying. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14226811461397509111" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer9173574949989609018">I started this book by audio and finished the last 30% in my living room reading and balling my freaking eyes out until 2:00 am. <br/><br/>This book is so much more than 5 stars, it makes me question most of my 5 star ratings because it just MORE. I loved this book on a level I can't describe. Bright Side made me grateful for the life I have been given, it broke my heart imagining the struggles of other people around me, and it made me want to be a better person. <br/><br/>Bright Side isn't just a book or a charact</span>
  <span id="freeText9173574949989609018" style="display:none">I started this book by audio and finished the last 30% in my living room reading and balling my freaking eyes out until 2:00 am. <br /><br />This book is so much more than 5 stars, it makes me question most of my 5 star ratings because it just MORE. I loved this book on a level I can't describe. Bright Side made me grateful for the life I have been given, it broke my heart imagining the struggles of other people around me, and it made me want to be a better person. <br /><br />Bright Side isn't just a book or a character, it's a way of life. I don't think I will ever forget this book, I am still crying hours later. I hope that when I am faced with such adversity I can have the dignity and grace of Bright Side. I hope that when I see others being mistreated I can have her compassion. I hope that when I begin to feel sorry for myself for things I cannot change I look on the Bright Side. This book...gah, it's just more. <br /><br />I hate reading sad books, but I also am so grateful that I took the time to let my heart break and enjoy this story!<br /><br />I can't wait to read Gus when my heart heals just a little!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9173574949989609018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1041508098" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1041508098" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1041508098?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22673436-bright-side">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1041508098" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5805340553628623515"><b>3.75 <i>Sunset</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"My life will not be a fairy tale, and that's okay. My life is reality."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492320418ra/22505086.gif' width='390' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>After very slowly reaching the 70 percent mark I had put this book aside feeling that the rest of the story would be anticlimax. <br/><br/>So many friends have read this book in full and just loved it so I went back in today. Upon my completion, I will say the overall message isn't anything we haven't heard or read before but somewhere in the delivery and beautiful way Katie touched those around her was. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"She'</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText5805340553628623515" style="display:none"><b>3.75 <i>Sunset</i> Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"My life will not be a fairy tale, and that's okay. My life is reality."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492320418ra/22505086.gif" width="390" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>After very slowly reaching the 70 percent mark I had put this book aside feeling that the rest of the story would be anticlimax. <br><br>So many friends have read this book in full and just loved it so I went back in today. Upon my completion, I will say the overall message isn't anything we haven't heard or read before but somewhere in the delivery and beautiful way Katie touched those around her was. <br><br><b>
  <i>"She's not the poster child for positivity. She's a freaking ray of sunshine. She doesn't just look on the bright side...she lives there."</i>
</b><br><br>The characters were very lovable while the pacing for me was so very slow. The ending is predictable and yes it's sad it was a good read. I would definitely read a book about Gus and I'm hoping that will be in the works someday.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Show time"</i>
</b><br><br> <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5805340553628623515" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1577254255" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577254255" />
    <a title="ȷαεlα" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16126654-l"><img alt="ȷαεlα" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589706072p2/16126654.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577254255?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ȷαεlα" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ȷαεlα" href="/user/show/16126654-l">ȷαεlα</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577254255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14958057676883706579"><b>
  <i>"If you start a book and a couple of chapters in you decide you just aren't into it that's one thing, but once you reach the halfway point, there's no turning back"</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>This books would probably have been a 4-4.5 star rating if it wasn't for its first 50%, which had me continuously<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457081049i/18315794.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>AND THE WORD <b>DUDE</b>, really!?? DUDE?? It shows up 195 times(<b>yes, I counted!!</b>).<br/>I hated every time one of the characters said "dude". I would add 2 more stars, but that effing word cheapened so much this book.<br/><br/>If I were to </span>
  <span id="freeText14958057676883706579" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"If you start a book and a couple of chapters in you decide you just aren't into it that's one thing, but once you reach the halfway point, there's no turning back"</i>
</b><br><br><br>This books would probably have been a 4-4.5 star rating if it wasn't for its first 50%, which had me continuously<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457081049i/18315794.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>AND THE WORD <b>DUDE</b>, really!?? DUDE?? It shows up 195 times(<b>yes, I counted!!</b>).<br>I hated every time one of the characters said "dude". I would add 2 more stars, but that effing word cheapened so much this book.<br><br>If I were to describe each half of the book with an expression, it would be like : 1st half-<b>WTF I AM READING!?</b> and the 2nd half-<b>COULD THIS BE MORE DRAMATIC?</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"A lot of happiness is bypassed, overlooked, postponed to a time years from now that may never come. Don't bide your time and miss out on this moment for a tomorrow with no guarantees."</i>
</b><br><br>*<b>
  <i>Ok, let's start. It contains major spoilers, so consider yourself warned.</i>
</b>*<br><br><br><b>1st half</b><br>Kate/Katherine/Bright side is a 19-20 old girl diagnosed with terminal cancer(<b>drama#1</b>). She had an older sister who had Down syndrome(<b>drama#2</b>), but died last year(<b>drama#3</b>). Her mother never loved her(<b>drama#4</b>) and she committed suicide(<b>drama#5</b>). Kate has a best friend named Gus, who is a rock star, who loves her, but doesn't say shit, because <i>she deserves someone better</i>. BUT, one night before Kate leaves home to go studying in Minnesota they have sex, but after that it's like nothing ever happened, still best buddies. They have slept(only slept and spooning many times), and this was pretty normal.-<i>Ewwww</i>, I can't even imagine spooning or just sleeping with my male friends, so awkward(It may happen sometimes when you're drunk or something, but all the time??Nahh). I would understand If there was going to happen anything else between them, but the author decides them to be eternally friends.<br>Then Kate meets some very special friends in Minnesota, (gay people, unsure people, sick people who don't think they're sick-<b>add more drama here</b>). She falls in love with a guy, who's a father in his 21 years, whose wife died 4 years ago, meaning he had his daughter when he was 15-16.(<i>Really</i>??!!-<b>more drama</b>.)<br><br>Kate is described as a sex diva, a drop dead gorgeous babe, even if she's 5 feet. Yeah, I know I'm being judgmental, but how is it possible to be realistic a friendship between her and a boy band of Viking Gods?! It's not just her appearance, but her personality. I know, life was shit to her, but come on! Gus thinks everyone falls for her in 5 min talking with her.<b>I didn't feel her Magic, sorry.</b> She isn't into romantic stuff, but for the situations in this book.<br><br>The way I imagine Kate is like a lesbian Macho woman. Her way of speaking made that possible, not my fault.<br><br><b>2nd half</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"But life doesn't come with a guarantee, Gus. We had 20 years together. That's pretty amazing when you think about it. And that friendship won't die with me, I know that. It will live inside you for the rest of your life. It's like a little piece of me gets to go on with you."</i>
</b><br><br>It was way better, but depressive. If I knew it, maybe I wouldn't finish this. There are people who like these kind of books, but they're not for me. Too much drama, suffering. Why did the author think it would be better for the book to have everything?(poverty, illness, gay, young father, sickness).Why couldn't she stick only to one plot? It would have been so much better. Oh, and add<b> music</b> to this for more diversity.<br><br>2 stars are more than enough. I am proud of myself for reading the first half, <i>DUDE</i>.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444170665ra/16461534.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14958057676883706579" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1040378982" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1040378982" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1040378982?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1040378982" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7077264666830670101"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409492703i/10985184._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5 ‘do epic ‘ stars</b><br/><br/><b>‘Regret just leads to second-guessing and anger and sadness and I sure as hell can’t afford any of those.’</b><br/><br/><b>I. AM. NUMB!</b> As I sit here<b> wiping the tears off my keyboard</b> I’m at a loss for words, and hours after finishing Bright Side, I’m still an emotional mess. This story made me swoon, it made my heart soar, it made me laugh, it made me sob, it devastated me and it inspired me and it <b>wrecked me!</b><br/><br/>I inhaled Bright Side in one sitting and when it was over, I was left staring into spa</span>
  <span id="freeText7077264666830670101" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409492703i/10985184._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5 ‘do epic ‘ stars</b><br><br><b>‘Regret just leads to second-guessing and anger and sadness and I sure as hell can’t afford any of those.’</b><br><br><b>I. AM. NUMB!</b> As I sit here<b> wiping the tears off my keyboard</b> I’m at a loss for words, and hours after finishing Bright Side, I’m still an emotional mess. This story made me swoon, it made my heart soar, it made me laugh, it made me sob, it devastated me and it inspired me and it <b>wrecked me!</b><br><br>I inhaled Bright Side in one sitting and when it was over, I was left staring into space and I’m not really sure how to adequately convey my thoughts and express my feelings. I experienced the whole gamut of emotions throughout this book which had me laughing one minute, swooning in romance heaven the next, and openly sobbing my heart out at the turn of a page. Kim Holden brought this powerful and breathtaking story to life and did it beautifully with heartfelt and gut wrenching emotion .<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m always looking forward toward the future…..I can’t afford not to. The future is all I have.”</i>
</b><br><br>I fell in love with all the characters, but Kate, Keller and Gus were something else. What special people they were. My heart alternated between overflowing with happiness and being completely annihilated and you know what? I wouldn’t have missed a second of it because when a book evokes that much emotion from you, you know you’re onto a winner.<br><br>For those who may be a bit hesitant to give this book a go, if you take a deep breath, open the page and allow yourself to be swept away you’ll be rewarded with spending time with some beautiful, memorable and unforgettable characters that will enter your heart and never leave. Yes, this story is gut wrenching and at times devastating, but it’s also inspiring, thought provoking and heart-warming.<br><br><b>‘I look forward to spending every minute I get to spend with her. Every minute of every day wouldn’t be enough.’</b><br><br>Friendship and love are at the forefront of this story and both the relationship between Gus and Kate and Kate and Keller are so beautifully portrayed, you experience both sides of Kate’s heart. Bright Sky is told through the pov’s of Kate and Keller, which only served to intensify the emotional impact of the story. There were times Keller’s pov broke me.<br><br>Kate was such a kind, positive, happy and accepting character. Despite not having the happiest of upbringings, Kate saw the good in everyone and everything; she was pure of heart and loyal and forgiving to a fault. She really does earn her nickname Bright Side. This extraordinary girl exudes a light and warmth that draws people to her and really possesses a truly beautiful soul. She owned my heart and she broke my heart.<br><br><b>‘What in the hell just happened? I feel like I’ve been asleep for years and I’ve only just woken up.’</b><br><br>Kate has been blessed with a unique and enduring friendship with her buddy Gus, an up and coming musician with his band Rook. It’s a friendship that has known happiness, pain, tragedy and loss and a shared connection brought about by their love of music cements a bond which is unbreakable. Gus owns a piece of Kate’s heart and I have to say, he owned a piece of mine too. He was such a beautiful big bear of a man and their friendship was so special.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Gus, it always gets better.”</i>
</b><br><br>Whilst Gus takes off to tour and establish his band, Kate starts a new life at College in Michigan. Kate knows where she’s heading and has a plan. It’s a plan that doesn’t include love, but somewhere along the way Keller Banks entered her life and threatens to shoot that plan to pieces.<br><br>Keller Banks. Well, words fail me on this beautiful, giving and completely selfless man. He was divine and I loved him! Keller was living a life pleasing others, never taking his own happiness into account, carrying secrets from his past that weighed him down. Katie entered his life like a bright shining star and knocked him for six.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I fell in love with you. It would’ve happened whether you loved me back or not. It’s impossible not to love you.” – Keller</i>
</b><br><br>I completely swooned over Kate and Keller’s relationship. It built at a slow and steady pace and I felt their connection deep in my bones. There was so much to Keller and as his and Kate’s secrets came to light, the true testament of this man and his character came to be. Arrgghhh Keller. I can’t think about him without crying. What a man!<br><br><b>
  <i>“You give me courage I never knew I had.” – Keller<br>“I didn’t do anything. It was there all along, you just had to find it.” – Kate</i>
</b><br><br>I connected to this book on many levels. There were times it did feel a bit cliché but at the end of the day these thoughts were soon forgotten and I find myself reflecting on the feelings I experienced and what a profound effect this book had on me. And it wasn’t just the characters and story I connected with in Bright Sky. This author clearly shares my passion for music and made it so it became an extension of her story as it wove through the pages.<br><br>I knew nothing going into this book and I’m thankful for that so I’m definitely not going to give anything away. I can’t say it enough about how this book made me <b>FEEL</b>. Grab some tissues (you’ll need them!) and <b>READ THIS BOOK!!.</b><br><br>This is one of those stories that hits your heart hard and carries messages that will leave you contemplating what’s important in life…you know… don’t sweat the small stuff. Be tolerant. Be forgiving. Open your heart and grab life by the scruff of the neck. Love hard, laugh often, follow your dreams and love life.<br><br><b>
  <i> “Thank you. I’m not really into the whole being rescued thing, but you make one helluva white knight, Keller Banks.”</i>
</b><br><br>I’m still a bit numb, so in the words of Katie….go forth and <b>‘do epic.’</b><br><br><br>✦✦✦<b> TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a></b> </span>
  <a data-text-id="7077264666830670101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who like light/funny ugly crying book</span></div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1033771920451427334"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461657090i/18891556.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Kate Sedgwick moved to a new small town for her college education.
