  <span id="freeText1033771920451427334" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461657090i/18891556.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kate Sedgwick moved to a new small town for her college education. With her bright, bubbly personality, she could charm just about anyone. Still, she never really opened up to anyone other than her best friend Gustov (Gus) Hawthorne.<br><br>Keller Banks was pretty hard to resist with his good looks and adoring personality. Both he and Kate were attracted to each other yet they tried to resist the pull because both of them have secrets big enough to push them apart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>While dark books feed my soul, the ugly crying ones are like sweet desserts haha! This book is definitely an ugly crier, but the beautiful thing is, it was also very light and funny.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>I’m an optimist, but first and foremost I’m a realist. My life will not follow a fairy tale, and that’s okay.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I adored Kate not only for her personality but also her strength. She lived up to her nickname Bright Side because she could put positive spin on anything that came her way.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“It scares me how much I like her. She makes me want to say screw it all and re-write my future.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Keller was also wonderful. I love how patient and understanding he was even though he had his low moments.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461657090i/18891557.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But my favorite was hands down Gus. He stole my heart from the moment he was first introduced. I love how much he cared about Kate and how much he didn't care about things that are not important in living a meaningful life.<br><br>The supporting characters were also equally lovable. Each of them brought something to the table besides just being entertaining. <br><br>What I love the most about this book is that it's not exactly a romance but rather a story about life. It's about living it to the fullest and not taking it for granted because life could easily take an unexpected turn.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>She’s refined the art of enjoyment and living in the moment. I’ve never seen anything like it. It’s breathtaking.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Bright Side is a story about love and friendship that endures through hardships in life. While heartbreaking at some points, the book is ultimately uplifting and heartwarming and hopefully will urge you to see things from a different perspective.<br><br><i><b>Note:</b><br>I don't have a personal experience in the subject matter so I don't know how I would cope being at either side of the story, but I know for sure it requires a lot of strength for all involved. </i><br><br><b>Standalone books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22669832.Bright_Side__Bright_Side___1_" title="Bright Side (Bright Side, #1) by Kim Holden" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1430743077s/23389993.jpg" alt="Gus (Bright Side, #2) by Kim Holden" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer5024215065163251706">So, I don't think I could ever pick a rating on this book. The numbers 1-5 are too simplistic of a way to describe my feelings on this book so I won't rate it. Don't know if I ever will.<br/><br/>I also don't really know how to review this, but I'll try and say something short. This book had exactly the opposite effect on me that it had on other readers. Instead of being uplifting, I found it so incredibly sad and after finishing it, it left me in such a depressed mood. Please do not read the spoiler tags</span>
  <span id="freeText5024215065163251706" style="display:none">So, I don't think I could ever pick a rating on this book. The numbers 1-5 are too simplistic of a way to describe my feelings on this book so I won't rate it. Don't know if I ever will.<br /><br />I also don't really know how to review this, but I'll try and say something short. This book had exactly the opposite effect on me that it had on other readers. Instead of being uplifting, I found it so incredibly sad and after finishing it, it left me in such a depressed mood. Please do not read the spoiler tags unless you really want to be spoiled.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I am a huge HEA person. Like I have to have it. And I know you could argue that the ending had happy moments and all that, but death of a loved one is hard, and honestly I hate sad books. THIS WAS SO FUCKING SAD I CANNOT STAND IT! Obviously there were hints at Bright Side's illness but this type of story is not my cup of tea.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I will say though I think Kim Holden is a great writer, and while I wouldn't classify this as a romance or new adult, she told this story in a beautiful and positive manner that was not easy to pull off. Will I read anything else by her? YES. On one condition <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ if it has a fucking happy ending. otherwise no  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />So thanks for reading my ramblings and word vomit. I honestly cannot write a coherent review after this book. </span>

    <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover"><img alt="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369044455p2/11672704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1039551663?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover">Donna ~ The Romance Cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1039551663" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13520979316907721928">Bright Side by Kim Holden<br/>5 breathtaking stars!!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Today, my life is awesome.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>This book is up there on my favourite reads of 2014, hell even up there on my favourite reads of ALL TIME! Yes it is seriously that good. This is a book that I couldn’t put down, not for one measly second. Once I started I couldn’t stop and once I had finished I was completely and utterly devastated. I was not ready for this book to end, I just wanted more.<br/><br/>The writing style is fluid, beautiful, emotional, cap</span>
  <span id="freeText13520979316907721928" style="display:none">Bright Side by Kim Holden<br />5 breathtaking stars!!!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Today, my life is awesome.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><br />This book is up there on my favourite reads of 2014, hell even up there on my favourite reads of ALL TIME! Yes it is seriously that good. This is a book that I couldn’t put down, not for one measly second. Once I started I couldn’t stop and once I had finished I was completely and utterly devastated. I was not ready for this book to end, I just wanted more.<br /><br />The writing style is fluid, beautiful, emotional, captivating, gut wrenching, all encompassing, this book takes you over, heart, mind, body and soul. The heroines motto in this book is “DO EPIC” and Kim Holden has “DONE EPIC.” This book is EPIC, do not be dissuaded by an innocuous cover, in fact this is a prime example of “never judge a book by it’s cover,” what is inside this cover is exquisite and deserves to be read, to be devoured and to be inhaled. This book is like an emotional vortex, it sucks you in, drowns you in emotions and feels and doesn’t let you free until the end. Have I said that this book is EPIC!! One more point on the cover though, once you have read the book you will appreciate it’s symbolism, I can see why the author did it and I can appreciate it whole heartedly. Just please, if you have a few spare dollars/pounds, pick up this book, you will not regret it.<br /><br />This is one emotional book, it is devastating but it is devastatingly perfect, but and this is a big but it is perfectly balanced with humour, wit an addictive storyline and some amazing characters. Not one character is superfluous to the story, they all have their part in bringing this story together.<br /><br />Kate aka as Bright Side lives up to her nick name, she always looks on the bright side of life (cue Monty Python music). She has had a really crap upbringing but she has never let it get to her. She has made the most of the crap that life has dealt her and is one of these people that puts everybody first. She is intelligent and super talented but all her aspirations were put on hold when life dealt her a hand that forced her to put those dreams aside for the time being. Kate was a beautiful character inside and out, she was adorable, selfless, giving, trusting, infectious, you couldn’t help but smile and be happy in her company. She had the knack of bringing the shyest person to life, her personality shone like the sun, everyone she touched felt her, she radiated, she really was Bright Side. Her saving grace in life has been her best friend and neighbour Gus.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I can’t let the bad consume me or it would eat me whole. The bad stays in the bad corner of my mind, I don’t let it through the door to mingle with good, because the bad is a goddamn party pooper.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Gus was adorable, he was the epitome of the perfect best friend. These two loved each other unconditionally, the lines of friendship having been blurred once these two were firmly putting their best friends label first even though at times you knew, ideally in another world, another scenario that these two were meant to be together. They were more than best friends. Gus was a guitarist and singer in a band, Kate was his muse, they batted off each other, her being musically oriented as well meant that these two made beautiful music together. Kate was shy so she just remained in the back ground, but all she wanted in life was for Gus to succeed and she would push him all the way. Gus needed his best friend, he needed the push and she was always there for him, just like he was for her.<br /><br />The story starts with Kate tackling one of her bucket list items, she always wanted to go to University, finally life had changed enough to make this possible and we see her start University life with a flourish. She picks her friends wisely, brings life, love and laughter to all she meets. This is where she meets Keller.<br /><br />Keller was another lost soul, his own history already leaving its mark. Having never opened his heart up it is unsurprising that Kate manages to break down his walls and defences. Kate is reticent to jump into a relationship, preferring to keep to just friends but there is something about Keller, he makes her feel, he makes her want to push her reservations aside, he makes her take the leap. These two were truly beautiful together and Keller embraced her friendship with Gus…eventually.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I didn’t do anything. It was there all along, you just had to find it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><br />And that is all I can say about this book…if I say anymore it will give too much away and that would be a travesty. All I can say is please, please read this book, give this newbie author a chance. Let the emotion and feels take you away for those few hours, learn some life lessons, be inspired, you will laugh, you will cry, you will swoon, but most of all you will feel. This is one book that has left its indelible mark on my heart, a book that I will champion from now on. Only a few books have made that impact and I am glad to add another to that list.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I don’t know if the speed limit in California is 95 miles an hour, because I realize you guys probably do things a little different there, but it’s only 65 here, which is about how fast you take f**king corners.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Kim Holden, all I can say is you are EPIC, this book is something that you should be truly proud of. I totally and utterly loved it and will now be eagerly anticipating your next book.<br /><br />Go and 1click peeps, you will not be disappointed.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theromancecover.com">www.theromancecover.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13520979316907721928" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1655285033" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1655285033" />
    <a title="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic"><img alt="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529028941p2/39243185.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1655285033?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" href="/user/show/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic">Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lovers of tear-jerkers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=grief">grief</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=bittersweet">bittersweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=illness">illness</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1655285033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1986425522483886796">I realize that I'm in the minority with giving this book below 5 stars but I couldn't help it. I'm a huge fan of a happily-ever-after. Nuff said.<br/><br/>As beautifully written as the story was, and it was beautiful, unfortunately my heart was broken beyond repair. And as much as I loved Gus, I can't find the will to read his book. Love should never die. Ever. Reading his book would be like contradicting that and I just can't.<br/><br/>Yes I loved Kate. Her personality made even me happy. Her relationship with Gus</span>
  <span id="freeText1986425522483886796" style="display:none">I realize that I'm in the minority with giving this book below 5 stars but I couldn't help it. I'm a huge fan of a happily-ever-after. Nuff said.<br /><br />As beautifully written as the story was, and it was beautiful, unfortunately my heart was broken beyond repair. And as much as I loved Gus, I can't find the will to read his book. Love should never die. Ever. Reading his book would be like contradicting that and I just can't.<br /><br />Yes I loved Kate. Her personality made even me happy. Her relationship with Gus left me envious even while I enjoyed and appreciated their bond. Her relationship with Keller... from their friendship to what they turned into... what they became... they made my heart sing.<br /><br />My thoughts: this book was bittersweet and full of heavy emotion. My heart feels... heavy. Those letters... the audio CD... I couldn't help but feel it deep. So while I love most everything about the story, I'm leaving my rating as is and hope my review clearly explains my reasoning.<br /><br />If you're looking for a book that attempts to squeeze out every drop of emotion from you, this one will do it.<br /><br />Happy reading! xo</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1311705686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1742230873378772400"><b>5 “And I still want to be Kate when I grow up” Stars<br/><br/><i>“GO, DO EPIC”</i></b><br/><br/>Buddy-read with this charming <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58818027-fares' rel='nofollow noopener'>boy who accepted to be my buddy-reads-partner for life and he totally has cheated on me already.</a><br/><br/><b>HOW I FEEL ABOUT THIS BOOK:</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486354811ra/21906726.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>FINALLY AFTER A MILLENIUM I HAVE WROTE A REVIEW. </b><br/><br/>*Takes a deep breath, cracks her fingers, close her eyes.* <br/><br/>I hope this review makes justice to the <b>EPICNESS</b> this story is. I am so nervous because this is a book I really want everyone to try out, but I feel my soul will break if som</span>
  <span id="freeText1742230873378772400" style="display:none"><b>5 “And I still want to be Kate when I grow up” Stars<br><br><i>“GO, DO EPIC”</i></b><br><br>Buddy-read with this charming <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58818027-fares" rel="nofollow noopener">boy who accepted to be my buddy-reads-partner for life and he totally has cheated on me already.</a><br><br><b>HOW I FEEL ABOUT THIS BOOK:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486354811ra/21906726.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>FINALLY AFTER A MILLENIUM I HAVE WROTE A REVIEW. </b><br><br>*Takes a deep breath, cracks her fingers, close her eyes.* <br><br>I hope this review makes justice to the <b>EPICNESS</b> this story is. I am so nervous because this is a book I really want everyone to try out, but I feel my soul will break if someone hates it.<br><br>This is one of the most bittersweet books you will ever find. I am not kidding. If you can’t believe you can be heart-wrenchingly crying while having a big smile on your face this book will prove you wrong. <br><br>If you are getting into this book with the expectation of a great epic romance, I am sorry you may be disappointed. This is the first time in an NA book were although I liked the romance it was not the main thing why I kept reading. I was invested in <b>FRIENDSHIPS, LIFE, CHARACTERS, KATE, FEELS, LOVE. <br><br>➽FRIENDSHIP</b><br>💛GUS. do I even need to say more?<br>💛I loved how we get a tight friendship between female &amp; male. But tbh my heart is also broken because hell I shipped them okay. <br>💛Kate’s friendship and tight bond with everyone. She was so kind and her interactions with everyone were so funny and they filled me with giddy feelings. <br>💛Shelly+Kate=Tight female friendship<br>💛Dance parties.<br><br><b>➽LIFE</b><br>💛This book has a great take on life.<br>💛<i>“I’m not saying you shouldn’t pursue dreams and goals. Just don’t forsake the present for the unknowns of the future. A lot of happiness is bypassed, overlooked, postponed to a time years from now that may never come. Don’t bide your time and miss out on this moment for a tomorrow with no guarantee.”</i><br>💛Kate’s way to view life was beautiful, it honestly made me fall in love with it a tiny bit. Which I really needed.<br>💛POSITIVITY. This books seriously shits rainbows and bright sides, there is no other way of explaining it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ which is funny because she is fucking dying and fuck fuck fuck. Why do shitty things need to happen to awesome people <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>💛<i>“Today, my life is awesome.<br>I don’t want to think about tomorrow.<br>Or the day after that.<br>So I repeat to myself: Today, my life is awesome.” </i><br>💛Kim is queen because fuck she punched my heart over and over with everything. I mean life is shit yet kim still made it look awesome.<br>💛<i>“Don't judge each other. We all have our own shit. Keep your eyes on yours and your nose out of everyone else's unless you're invited in. And when you get the invitation, help, don't judge.”</i> <br><br><b>➽CHARACTERS</b><br>💛GUS: He is my fucking sunshine. I am so in love with him, I mean maybe not as much as I was with Kate in this book, but for sure he is my weakness. HOT, MUSICIAN, WONDERFUL HUMAN BEING. His interactions with Kate made my day, I just loved both so much. <br>💛SHELLY: She is wonderful. So tough but at the same time sweet as candy. And a great dancer, shhhh don’t tell her I told you.<br>💛KELLER: I wanna protect him from all dead in the world. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ FUCK HOW DO YOU MOVE ON FROM HAVING THE TWO WOMEN YOU LOVED DIE???? HOW??? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He was sarcastic, flirty, hot. <br>💛CLAY: I want to make him a magic poison against all those homophobic assholes in the world. He was funny and enthusiastic, basically lovely. <br>💛PETER: “a role-playing sex addict that gets off on S&amp;M.” “wearing only leather chaps and holding a riding crop...” *shakes head* THANK GUS, that picture is just. No, but in all seriousness, I loved his small sweet romance with the nerdy girl.<br>💛STELLA: Love her. Sweetest thing ever. <br><br><b>➽KATE</b><br>💛Yes, I am extra, yes she needed her own section apart from the other characters.<br>💛I LOVE HER. I LOVE HER. I LOVE HER.<br>💛Biggest crush I have ever had on a female character<br>💛<i>"dude"</i><br>💛Because she loves coffee black, books, underrated music, dancing.<br>💛Every time she smiled the whole room shined.<br>💛Open-minded goddess.<br>💛<i>“I know it’s weird, but I like to think of God as my homeboy.”</i> She made me want to talk with the big guy and I am NOT religious.<br>💛She is a great, brave friend.<br>💛<i>“You deserve someone who takes you out on real dates. Someone who buys you flowers and shit. Because if there's anyone in this world who's capable of insane amounts of love and who deserves to be loved that way in return, it's you.” </i><br>💛JUST A WONDERFUL PERSON. <br><br><b>➽FEELS</b><br>💛I laughed like crazy.<br>💛I cried like there was no tomorrow.<br>💛The quotes, the quotes, the quotes.<br>💛If you didn’t feel anything you are made of stone.<br>💛Twix bars (If you get this reference I love you)<br><br><b>➽LOVE</b><br>💛Love for life<br>💛Love for friendship<br>💛Love for love<br>💛Love for oneself<br>💛<b>LOVE THIS BOOK</b><br>💛Love for Kim Holden because she created this book, like how?<br><br>If you still haven’t got the clue, <b>I LOVE THIS BOOK.</b> So yeah, now is your decision if you wanna make your life a better place by reading this book or not. But yeah not to hype the book or anything.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1650278860" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1650278860" />
    <a title="Andie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30510075-andie"><img alt="Andie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477111902p2/30510075.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1650278860?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andie " href="/user/show/30510075-andie">Andie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=all-the-feels">all-the-feels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1650278860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17762282369977788184">I decided to pick up <i> Bright Side </i> after hearing many gushing reviews and being recommended as a tearjerker. I was in need of a good cry so this was a no brainer. But it's SO much more than that. This story has moved and inspired me. I'm not going to talk about the plot whatsoever because that's for everyone to discover and enjoy on their own. <br/><br/>In all honesty, I was moving pretty slowly at first. I wasn't sure where the story was going, if anywhere. Then close to halfway... BAM! Everything is put</span>
  <span id="freeText17762282369977788184" style="display:none">I decided to pick up <i> Bright Side </i> after hearing many gushing reviews and being recommended as a tearjerker. I was in need of a good cry so this was a no brainer. But it's SO much more than that. This story has moved and inspired me. I'm not going to talk about the plot whatsoever because that's for everyone to discover and enjoy on their own. <br /><br />In all honesty, I was moving pretty slowly at first. I wasn't sure where the story was going, if anywhere. Then close to halfway... BAM! Everything is put into perspective. What and where the story is leading and why we had the lead up that we did. <i> Bright Side </i> is Kate's story. A girl made of sunshine and rainbows and unicorns. She's an extremely positive, live in the moment, fly by the seat of your pants kind of girl. She doesn't just look on the bright side, she lives there. And girl is <b> BRAVE </b>! No one can help but fall in love with her. The lead up and all the details are so vital in the end. By the time I finished the book its wasn't just a story anymore. I felt like I knew each of these characters as if they were my own friends and family. I felt right along with them.<br /><br />The love interest, Keller is a wonderful character and fits with Kate beautifully. As much as Kate didn't want to get attached to anyone, Keller was just as good for her as she was for him. But the real star of the show here is Kate's lifelong best friend, Gus. I'm so thankful for all the build up to get to know his beautiful soul. I can't wait to read the follow up, <i> Gus </i> soon. <br /><br />If you're looking for a hit you in the feels yet highly uplifting read, I urge you to pick up <i> Bright Side </i>. And if you find yourself questioning the momentum of the story like I was, don't give up! I promise it's all worth it in the end. <br /><br />Do like Kate and <b> do epic </b>!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17762282369977788184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1041942016" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1041942016" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1041942016?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780991140244" href="/book/show/23361701-bright-side">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=books-that-cross-the-line">books-that-cross-the-line</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1041942016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5898880912170396128">The heart of this book is to never take anything for granted. Enjoy every moment...every hug and every kiss, bask in the good and lessen the bad. And you never really realize the impact you have on those around you. <br/><br/>And the <b>heart</b> of this book is all things Kate. She epitomizes everything I just said...and that's saying a lot. She's had a horrible childhood but her saving grace was her sister, Gracie, and her best friend, Gus. Now, she's moved to Minnesota for college and to get a fresh start.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413768288ra/11560350.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  </b></span>
  <span id="freeText5898880912170396128" style="display:none">The heart of this book is to never take anything for granted. Enjoy every moment...every hug and every kiss, bask in the good and lessen the bad. And you never really realize the impact you have on those around you. <br><br>And the <b>heart</b> of this book is all things Kate. She epitomizes everything I just said...and that's saying a lot. She's had a horrible childhood but her saving grace was her sister, Gracie, and her best friend, Gus. Now, she's moved to Minnesota for college and to get a fresh start.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413768288ra/11560350.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>(Thanks Jeanne for the gif!)</i>
</b><br><br>In the beginning, the book is s-l-o-w. It's written in a day by day format, so it takes a while for things to start happening. At first, it was a little boring but then I realized that we needed to <i>really</i> know Kate and what she was about. Also, there's a lot we don't know and that drove me crazy. <br><br>Add to the mix a great group of characters...some of my favorites are:<br><br>Gus is her best friend and has grown up with Kate. They have a lot in common and you soon find out the depths of Gus' feelings. It's hard not to pull for him but...it's complicated. I really enjoyed him but I was going to scream every time she wrote about him smoking...enough already! <br><br>Keller becomes very important to Kate. I loved seeing how their relationship developed but he has some secrets of his own. My heart went out to him though to have to go through it x2. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413927400i/11582514.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>("It's showtime.")</i>
</b> <br><br>I wish we had gotten to know more about Shelly? She also has some secrets but I loved how Kate was chipping away at things. <br><br>Clayton was a real sweetie. I felt horrible at the things he went through but I was glad Kate was there for him. And Morris was too.<br><br>So what about the romance and the steaminess? Well, I can only tell u a bit about it...just suffix it to say there is <i>some</i>. I would've like a lot more but it is what it is. I do think having the different POVs helped to get more understanding of the feelings involved. <br><br>And that leaves us with this: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/552271.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>or maybe this is you...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/511079.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>then again, you might just feel like this...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414102229ra/11608623.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I think most people will get <i>at least</i> a little teary eyed. <br><br>Overall, I enjoyed it and would definitely recommend it if you want an emotional read. There is another book coming out in 2015...<i>
  <b>I won't say who it's about since it was a spoiler for me</b>
</i> but I'm definitely looking forward to it! <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/618217.gif" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "Dude, you haven't been replaced. No one spoons like you do."<br><br>♥ "Facebook is the decline of civilization as we know it."<br><br>♥ "Goddammit, Bright Side, I think the big boy pants worked."<br><br>♥ "You are brave."<br><br>♥ "Do epic."<br><br>♥ "She doesn't just look on the bright side. She lives there."<br><br><br>♦ BR w/the BR group! </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1936214237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9625087979212678334">Kate grew up believing that she needed to take care of everybody...[her mother, sister, friends, strangers],...<br/>She had an exceptional disposition about life... with no regrets. Tragedies included. <br/><br/>A 20 year best friend relationship, a passionate ‘in-love’ relationship, college friends,<br/>music, and values on life,<br/>are at the heart of this story.<br/><br/>Sappy - sweet - sad - <br/>- intimate storytelling! <br/><br/>This is another one of those books where I can understand high rating reviews — and low ones.<br/>Readers can choos</span>
  <span id="freeText9625087979212678334" style="display:none">Kate grew up believing that she needed to take care of everybody...[her mother, sister, friends, strangers],...<br />She had an exceptional disposition about life... with no regrets. Tragedies included. <br /><br />A 20 year best friend relationship, a passionate ‘in-love’ relationship, college friends,<br />music, and values on life,<br />are at the heart of this story.<br /><br />Sappy - sweet - sad - <br />- intimate storytelling! <br /><br />This is another one of those books where I can understand high rating reviews — and low ones.<br />Readers can choose to see the bright side of Kate’s attributes —<br />or—<br />readers could possibly feel she was too upbeat to be unbelievable. <br /><br />I’m choosing the bright side.<br />It’s not often I read about a main character who is sincerely selfless as Kate was. <br />One of her greatest gifts, was that she was genuinely interested in listening to others. <br /><br />Kate knew how to make other people feel great about themselves....a gift I deeply admire in others. <br /><br />Easy listening Audiobook...<br />It’s not rocket science. <br />It’s a chick read.<br /><br />If you hate sappy - don’t choose this book.<br />Me... I like a little sappy from time to time!<br />....Besides it was a side-tribute to ‘black’ coffee. Ha! For a tea drinker - I understand this from Paul - ‘a black’ coffee guy, too! <br /><br />Thank you, Gina!<br />You’re a sweetheart ... and it was nice being with this book - thinking of you!</span>

<div id="review_1042510159" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1042510159" />
    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1042510159?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780991140244" href="/book/show/23361701-bright-side">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=book-husband">book-husband</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=music">music</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=tears-and-more-tears">tears-and-more-tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-fictional-boyfriends">my-fictional-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-favorite-book-ever">my-favorite-book-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1042510159" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14251460034329922851"><b>*****5++ Epic Stars*****</b><br/><br/>If this book were a person I would want to hug it so, so hard, maybe even go on vacations with it, go dancing and even tell it all of my secrets. <i>Bight Side</i> is a beautiful and uplifting story that I will never, ever forget. <3<br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/a49b875a-b254-46b6-a0c6-c621fe65a01f_zpsjw5ruhjp.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431466422i/14839499.jpg' alt=' photo a49b875a-b254-46b6-a0c6-c621fe65a01f_zpsjw5ruhjp.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Kate Sedgwick is the kind of girl who lives her life on the <i>Bright Side</i>, always looking for the positive in every situation and every person. She has known the meaning of pain from a very young age but instead of using it as an excuse to become j</span>
  <span id="freeText14251460034329922851" style="display:none"><b>*****5++ Epic Stars*****</b><br><br>If this book were a person I would want to hug it so, so hard, maybe even go on vacations with it, go dancing and even tell it all of my secrets. <i>Bight Side</i> is a beautiful and uplifting story that I will never, ever forget. &lt;3<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/a49b875a-b254-46b6-a0c6-c621fe65a01f_zpsjw5ruhjp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431466422i/14839499.jpg" alt=" photo a49b875a-b254-46b6-a0c6-c621fe65a01f_zpsjw5ruhjp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kate Sedgwick is the kind of girl who lives her life on the <i>Bright Side</i>, always looking for the positive in every situation and every person. She has known the meaning of pain from a very young age but instead of using it as an excuse to become jaded and bitter towards life and people, she has learned from the bad and has used it to embraced life to the fullest. Her best friend Gus is a total rockstar, he is the one that brings music, support and love into her life. Kate and Gus grew up in San Diego, California and have always been inseparable but their careers are now taking them in different directions; Kate is going to college in Minnesota and Gus will be touring the US with his band to promote their music.<br><br>Their friendship is so beautiful and intense that is hard not to think of them as more than best friends but this love they share is at a higher level, is completely selfless, they live for one another and they would never allow anything or anybody to come between them. Gus is a sexy rock God, he's sweet and sensitive and the most important things for him are his girl Kate and his music.<br><br>The first part of the book is slow paced but in my head it makes sense that the author wrote that way because is in that part of the book where you will fall in love with Kate. Every person she comes in contact with she impacts in a deep and meaningful way. She will go down in history as one of my favorite heroines ever. Her character will get under your skin and by the time you finish reading this book you will feel like she is your friend. <br><br>Kate's black coffee addiction will take her into a coffee shop where she meets a brilliant man and sexy man, named Keller Banks. From the moment they meet the sparks fly, both are hiding life altering secrets that will both brake them and heal them at the same time. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/96c378d8-60f8-4863-ac64-f960b3ffc902_zpsn7tmkjtw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431466422i/14839500.jpg" alt=" photo 96c378d8-60f8-4863-ac64-f960b3ffc902_zpsn7tmkjtw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I truly fell in love with every character in this story; also the beautiful writing style and the inspiring plot took over my heart and made it fly into a world where friendship is the balm that heals all wounds. This book is about love and celebrating every moment and every person in our lives. Kate shares her enthusiasm and joy for life in a way that will leave you with no choice but to think about your own life and ways to improve it.<br><br><i>Bright Side</i> is truly a transcendent story that I think everyone should read. I must admit I cried and did it hard and with purpose but every tear was totally worth it. I love that if I ever find myself missing Kate and her encouraging rules and wit, I can always go back to my book and dance and sing and do epic, with her.<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/41026564-495c-4d2e-a353-ecf52fca8641_zpse2bi0n24.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431466422i/14839501.jpg" alt=" photo 41026564-495c-4d2e-a353-ecf52fca8641_zpse2bi0n24.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br> My<i>Bright Side</i>music playlist:<br>*Hold Back The River by James Bay<br>*Closer by Tegan and Sara<br>*When You Sleep by Mary Lambert<br>*Need The Sun to Break by James Bay<br>*Medicine by Sunset Sons</span>
  <a data-text-id="14251460034329922851" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1074594979" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1074594979" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1074594979?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1074594979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3308591290851645843">This is the story of Kate. Kate and the world that she creates around her, the world that makes your life a little bit better because you know her. Because she smiled at you and it brightened your day. It’s a story about life, love and friendship. About being brave and living the life you were given; making the best of it. No matter what. <br/><br/>Kate is heading to Minnesota from sunny California to attend college. Leaving behind Gus, her best friend for the Grant College Experience. *Fist Pump* Between</span>
  <span id="freeText3308591290851645843" style="display:none">This is the story of Kate. Kate and the world that she creates around her, the world that makes your life a little bit better because you know her. Because she smiled at you and it brightened your day. It’s a story about life, love and friendship. About being brave and living the life you were given; making the best of it. No matter what. <br /><br />Kate is heading to Minnesota from sunny California to attend college. Leaving behind Gus, her best friend for the Grant College Experience. *Fist Pump* Between attending classes, making friends, consuming coffee and falling in love; Kate harbors her own secret. One that she isn’t ready to tell. Not until she has to. <br /><br />When you hear whispers of a book coming from the mouths of a handful of authors and you see things like “life changing” being mentioned in the comments from readers, you just know you have to read this. Then you do a little more recon, cause you still have no idea what this book is about, you just know that it is going to be epic. But you don’t read the reviews because there is that nagging voice that tells you that someone might spoil it. And you know that half the torture is being destroyed by a book. So you buy it. And if you’re like me, you stare at it for a few weeks before you muster up the courage to read it. So I finally reached that point, where I had to start it. Then it happened. I couldn’t put it down. <br /><br />It was tragic, it was beautiful. It was life changing. It’s one of those books that makes you reevaluate your life and what is important. Causes you to remember not to sweat the small stuff and to find the bright side of the darkest of times. To embrace life and the moments that take your breath away, because you’ll need them when you reach the moments that make it harder to breath.<br /><br />The characters. Every.Single.One. Loved them. Even Maddie served the right purpose. But the main characters; Kate, Gus &amp; Keller. Blew me away. Kate, I wanted to be her when I grow up. I want to find my own inner Kate. Each character in this holds a piece of my heart and will for years to come. When I look at the list of books that I’ve read and think about what I took away from each of those stories, there is no doubt that this book will top that list every time. <br /><br />An instant favorite. No doubts about it. I don’t know if I can ever read it again, but I do know that there will be times that will come down the road when I think about this book and the lessons it teaches. I don’t think there will come a time when thinking about this story won’t bring me to tears. <br /><br />Be brave, do epic. Watch a sunset and cheer because you experienced its beauty. Love your friends hard and befriend those that look like they need it the most. Stand up for those that haven’t yet realized they deserve it and show them they do. Give them the courage to stand up for themselves. Live your life with a smile because you only get one life. <br /><br />Knowing that Gus is going to get his book makes my heart smile. I cannot wait to have his story. I need to have his book. I don’t think there is a story that needs to be told more than this one. Ever. <br /><br />Read this. Now. It will impact you, you can’t escape it. I find it difficult sometimes to recommend a book to fellow readers because even when we share the same opinion of one book, we can often disagree on so many others. But this book, this one... well this is one that I have no reservations about. This is one of those books that makes me want to buy handful of paperback books and just leave them in random places so people can find them and read it. <br /><br /><i> Images coming soon </i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3308591290851645843" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('uzZw7LmqPwWNysHBxhXTVHhghkWFpGAhrrH7l50cgW9SVdjbHm93ph/6l/eBMHPC5ZPQEzUGPfoz2xOmha6j2A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('g9ixo7UhiXvod3otgUoGW8TRCcESuRlreVBvOf17DKJquxmUEuTB2HpHLBvGb6bNWSJfl6IbRLDkOocI5ckuFQ==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer12069415031118872300">Some of my favorite things: reading, writing, the two coolest guys on the planet (my husband and son), my bicycle (my husband built it for me), Facebook (I'm fairly certain it's an addiction at this point), iced coffee (hazelnut), and music (LOVE Sunset Sons, the 1975, Dredg, the xx, Balance and Composure, Teenage Bottlerocket, and 30 Seconds to Mars). I also love dreaming, which brings me to my n</span>
  <span id="freeText12069415031118872300" style="display:none">Some of my favorite things: reading, writing, the two coolest guys on the planet (my husband and son), my bicycle (my husband built it for me), Facebook (I'm fairly certain it's an addiction at this point), iced coffee (hazelnut), and music (LOVE Sunset Sons, the 1975, Dredg, the xx, Balance and Composure, Teenage Bottlerocket, and 30 Seconds to Mars). I also love dreaming, which brings me to my next point. I have one bit of advice for anyone reading this ... follow your dreams. It's never too late. Get started today ... heck get started RIGHT NOW! I wanted to write a book 20 years ago. Instead I waited. And waited. I should've been writing. But I didn't. I don't do regrets, because the past is just that, the past. But let me tell you there's nothing in the world like achieving something you've dreamt about for years and years. So, get started. Make your dreams reality. <br />I love to hear from other readers. Send me a message or find me on Facebook (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://facebook.com/kimholdenauthor">https://facebook.com/kimholdenauthor</a>) and tell what's up in your reading world.</span>
